                    <h2 class="Uo8X3b OhScic zsYMMe">Featured snippet from the web</h2>

                    <div>

                     <div>

                      <div class="yp1CPe wDYxhc NFQFxe viOShc LKPcQc" data-md="471" lang="en-NZ">

                       <div class="V3FYCf">

                        <div class="wDYxhc" data-md="61" lang="en-NZ" style="clear:none">

                         <div class="LGOjhe" data-attrid="wa:/description" aria-level="3" role="heading" data-hveid="CBIQAA">

                          <span class="ILfuVd" lang="en"><span class="hgKElc">Software testing is <b>the process of evaluating and verifying that a software product or application does what it is supposed to do</b>. The benefits of testing include preventing bugs, reducing development costs and improving performance.</span></span>

                         </div>

                       <div class="di3YZe">

                        <div class="co8aDb" aria-level="3" role="heading">

                         <b>Let's dig into these sequential phases of the software testing life cycle:</b>

                        </div>

                        <div class="RqBzHd">

                         <ul class="i8Z77e">

                          <li class="TrT0Xe">Requirement analysis.</li>

                          <li class="TrT0Xe">Test planning.</li>

                          <li class="TrT0Xe">Test case design and development.</li>

                          <li class="TrT0Xe">Test environment setup.</li>

                          <li class="TrT0Xe">Test execution.</li>

                          <li class="TrT0Xe">Test cycle closure.</li>

                         </ul>

                        </div>

                        <div class="RqBzHd">

                          <li class="TrT0Xe">Integration Testing.</li>

                          <li class="TrT0Xe">System Testing.</li>

                          <li class="TrT0Xe">Functional Testing.</li>

                          <li class="TrT0Xe">Acceptance Testing.</li>

                          <li class="TrT0Xe">Smoke Testing.</li>

                          <li class="TrT0Xe">Regression Testing.</li>

                          <li class="TrT0Xe">Performance Testing.</li>

                  <div jsname="bVEB4e" class="wWOJcd" aria-controls="exacc_kafmY5T_H52P2roP_Jy8gAU_2" aria-expanded="false" aria-labelledby="exacc_kafmY5T_H52P2roP_Jy8gAU_1" role="button" tabindex="0" jsaction="AWEk5c">

                    <span>What are the 5 testing methods?</span>

                   </div>

                   <div jsname="Q8Kwad" class="YsGUOb"></div>

                   <div jsname="K8Pnod" class="r21Kzd" data-hveid="CEUQAQ" data-ved="2ahUKEwjUi5GT5Iv9AhWdh1YBHXwOD1AQuk56BAhFEAE"></div>

                   <div jsname="Fus96e" class="guvigf" data-ved="2ahUKEwjUi5GT5Iv9AhWdh1YBHXwOD1AQ36YDegQIRRAC"></div>

                  </div>

                  <div jsname="rozPHf" class="MBtdbb" id="exacc_kafmY5T_H52P2roP_Jy8gAU_2" data-ved="2ahUKEwjUi5GT5Iv9AhWdh1YBHXwOD1AQ7NUEegQIRRAD">

                   <div class="ymu2Hb" jsslot="">

                    <div jsname="oQYOj" class="t0bRye r2fjmd" id="_kafmY5T_H52P2roP_Jy8gAU_47" data-hveid="CEUQBA" data-ved="2ahUKEwjUi5GT5Iv9AhWdh1YBHXwOD1AQu04oAHoECEUQBA">

                     <div id="kafmY5T_H52P2roP_Jy8gAU__63">

                      <div class="wDYxhc" data-md="83">

                       <div class="di3YZe">

                        <div class="co8aDb" aria-level="3" role="heading">

                         <b>There are many different types of testing, but for this article we will stick to the core five components of testing:</b>

                        </div>

                        <div class="RqBzHd">

                         <ul class="i8Z77e">

                          <li class="TrT0Xe">1) Unit Tests. ... </li>

                          <li class="TrT0Xe">2) Integration/System Tests. ... </li>

                          <li class="TrT0Xe">3) Functional Tests. ... </li>

                          <li class="TrT0Xe">4) Regression Tests. ... </li>

                          <li class="TrT0Xe">5) Acceptance Tests.</li>

                         </ul>

                         <div class="u9iNfb">

                          <div class="Od5Jsd">

                           6/06/2017

                          </div>

                         </div>
